</head>
<body>
    <h1>My Borrowings</h1>
    {% if borrowings %}
    <table border="1" id="borrowings-table">
        <thead>
            <tr>
                <th>Book Title</th>
                <th>Borrow Date</th>
                <th>Due Date</th>
                <th>Status</th>
                <th>Actions</th>
            </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
            {% for borrow in borrowings %}
            <tr>
                <td>{{ borrow.book_title }}</td>
                <td>{{ borrow.borrow_date }}</td>
                <td>{{ borrow.due_date }}</td>
                <td>{{ borrow.status }}</td>
                <td>
                    {% if borrow.status == 'Active' %}
                    <form action="{{ url_for('return_book', borrow_id=borrow.borrow_id) }}" method="POST" style="display:inline;">
                        <button type="submit" id="return-book-button-{{ borrow.borrow_id }}">Return</button>
                    </form>
                    {% else %}
                    <button disabled>Return</button>
                    {% endif %}
                </td>
            </tr>
            {% endfor %}
        </tbody>
    </table>
    {% else %}
    <div id="no-borrowings-message">You have no borrowings yet.</div>
    {% endif %}
    <button onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'" id="back-to-dashboard">Back to Dashboard</button>
</body>

# OnlineLibrary Comprehensive Test Report

## 1. Functional Testing

### Borrow Book Workflow
- Tested borrowing of book with ID 2 (Sapiens) which was initially Available.
- Borrowing succeeded with success=True and confirmation message.
- Book status updated from Available to Borrowed.
- borrowings.txt updated correctly with valid borrow record.

*Details:* First borrowing record in borrowings.txt matches user and book IDs.

## 2. UI Verification
- Verified all HTML templates against design_spec.md requirements.
- All required element IDs are present and correctly used as per spec.
- Dynamic content rendered with Jinja2 syntax consistent with backend variables.
- Navigation links on buttons correctly use `url_for` with proper endpoints.

## 3. Data Integrity
- Initial data files loaded correctly.
- Borrowing operation updated books.txt and borrowings.txt consistently without corruption.
- Temporary test data cleared after test.

## 4. Issues
- None found during simulated borrow test and UI verification.

## Conclusion
- Critical borrow workflow functional and data integrity verified.
- UI meets specifications.

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <title>{{ book.title }} - Details</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="/static/styles.css">
</head>
<body>
    <div id="book-details-page">
        <h1 id="book-title">{{ book.title }}</h1>
        <div id="book-author"><strong>Author:</strong> {{ book.author }}</div>
        <div id="book-description">
            <p>{{ book.description }}</p>
        </div>
        <div id="book-status"><strong>Status:</strong> {{ book.status }}</div>
        <button id="back-to-catalog" onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('book_catalog') }}'">Back to Catalog</button>
        {% if book.status == 'Available' %}
            <button id="borrow-button" onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('borrow_confirmation', book_id=book.book_id) }}'">Borrow</button>
        {% else %}
            <button id="borrow-button" disabled>Borrow</button>
        {% endif %}
    </div>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <title>Borrow Confirmation</title>
</head>
<body>
    <div id="borrow-page">
        <div id="borrow-book-info">
            <h2>{{ book.title }}</h2>
            <div>Author: {{ book.author }}</div>
            <div>Status: {{ book.status }}</div>
        </div>
        <div id="due-date-display">Due Date: {{ due_date }}</div>
        <form method="POST" action="{{ url_for('confirm_borrow', book_id=book.book_id) }}">
            <button id="confirm-borrow-button" type="submit">Confirm Borrow</button>
            <button id="cancel-borrow-button" type="button" onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('book_details', book_id=book.book_id) }}'">Cancel</button>
        </form>
    </div>

=== /home/jun/0624/CaMP_0327_backup/results/Software-web-rebuttal/compound_maxfailover_3/OnlineLibrary/compound_chaos/templates/catalog.html ===
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <title>Book Catalog</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="/static/styles.css">
</head>
<body>
    <div id="catalog-page">
        <h1>Book Catalog</h1>
        <input type="text" id="search-input" placeholder="Search books..." oninput="filterBooks()">
        <select id="filter-status">
            <option value="All">All Statuses</option>
            <option value="Available">Available</option>
            <option value="Borrowed">Borrowed</option>
            <option value="Reserved">Reserved</option>
        </select>
        <div id="book-grid">
            {% for book in books %}
                <div class="book-card">
                    <h2>{{ book.title }}</h2>
                    <div>Author: {{ book.author }}</div>
                    <div>Status: {{ book.status }}</div>
                    <button onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('book_details', book_id=book.book_id) }}'">View Details</button>
                </div>
            {% endfor %}
        </div>
        <button id="dashboard-button" onclick="window.location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Dashboard</button>
    </div>
    <script>
        function filterBooks() {
            const searchInput = document.getElementById('search-input').value.toLowerCase();
            const statusFilter = document.getElementById('filter-status').value;
            const books = document.getElementById('book-grid').children;
            for (let book of books) {
                const title = book.querySelector('h2').textContent.toLowerCase();
                const status = book.querySelector('div:nth-child(3)').textContent.replace('Status: ', '');
                const matchesSearch = title.includes(searchInput);
                const matchesStatus = (statusFilter === 'All') || (status === statusFilter);
                if (matchesSearch && matchesStatus) {
                    book.style.display = '';
                } else {
                    book.style.display = 'none';
                }
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>
